replaceable units, including replacement of whole engines or engine modules.\n\n\n9E001\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\"Technology\" according to the General Technology Note for the \"development\" of equipment or \"software\", specified in 9A001.b., 9A004 to 9A012, 9A350, 9B or 9D.\n\n\n9E002\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\"Technology\" according to the General Technology Note for the \"production\" of equipment specified in 9A001.b., 9A004 to 9A011, 9A350 or 9B.\n\n\nN.B.:\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0For \"technology\" for the repair of controlled structures, laminates or materials, see 1E002.f.\n\n\n9E003\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Other \"technology\" as follows:\n\n\na.\"Technology\" \"required\" for the \"development\" or \"production\" of any of the following gas turbine engine components or systems:\n\n\n1.Gas turbine blades, vanes or \"tip shrouds\", made from directionally solidified (DS) or single crystal (SC) alloys and having (in the 001Miller Index Direction) a stress-rupture life exceeding 400 hours at 1,273 K (1000 \u00b0C) at a stress of 200 MPa, based on the average property values;\n\n\n2.Combustors having any of the following:\n\n\na.Thermally decoupled liners designed to operate at 'combustor exit temperature' exceeding 1883 K (1610 \u00b0C);\n\n\nb.Non-metallic liners;\n\n\n\n\nc.Non-metallic shells; or\n\n\nd.Liners designed to operate at 'combustor exit temperature' exceeding 1883 K (1610 \u00b0C) and having holes that meet the parameters specified by 9E003.c.;\n\n\nNote:The \"required\" \"technology\" for holes in 9E003.a.2. is limited to the derivation of the geometry and location of the holes.\n\n\nTechnical Note:\n\n\n'Combustor exit temperature' is the bulk average gas path total (stagnation) temperature between the combustor exit plane and the leading edge of the turbine inlet guide vane (i.e., measured at engine station T40 as defined in SAE ARP 755A) when the engine is running in a 'steady state mode' of operation at the certificated maximum continuous operating temperature.\n\n\nN.B.:See 9E003.c. for \"technology\" \"required\" for manufacturing cooling holes.\n\n\n3.Components that are any of the following:\n\n\na.Manufactured from organic \"composite\" materials designed to operate above 588 K (315 \u00b0C);\n\n\nb.Manufactured from any of the following:\n\n\n1.Metal \"matrix\" \"composites\" reinforced by any of the following:\n\n\na.Materials specified in 1C007;\n\n\nb.\"Fibrous or filamentary materials\" specified in 1C010; or\n\n\nc.Aluminides specified in 1C002.a.; or\n\n\n2.Ceramic \"matrix\" \"composites\" specified in 1C007.; or\n\n\nc.Stators, vanes, blades, tip seals (shrouds), rotating blings, rotating blisks, or 'splitter ducts', that are all of the following:\n\n\n1.Not specified in 9E003.a.3.a.;\n\n\n2.Designed for compressors or fans; and\n\n\n3.Manufactured from material specified in 1C010.e. with resins specified in 1C008;\n\n\nTechnical Note:\n\n\nA 'splitter duct' performs the initial separation of the air-mass flow between the bypass and core sections of the engine.\n\n\n\n\n4.Uncooled turbine blades, vanes or \"tip-shrouds\", designed to operate at a 'gas path temperature' of 1373 K (1100 \u00b0C) or more\n\n\n5.Cooled turbine blades, vanes, \"tip-shrouds\" other than those described in 9E003.a.1., designed to operate at a 'gas path temperature' of 1693 K (1420 \u00b0C) or more;\n\n\nTechnical Notes:\n\n\n1.'Gas path temperature' is the bulk average gas path total (stagnation) temperature at the leading edge plane of the turbine component when the engine is running in a 'steady state mode' of operation at the certificated or specified maximum continuous operating temperature.\n\n\n2.The term 'steady state mode' defines engine operation conditions, where the engine parameters, such as thrust/power, rpm and others, have no appreciable fluctuations, when the ambient air temperature and pressure at the engine inlet are constant.\n\n\n6.Airfoil-to-disk blade combinations using solid state joining;\n\n\n7.Gas turbine engine components using \"diffusion bonding\" \"technology\" specified in 2E003.b.;\n\n\n8.'Damage tolerant' gas turbine engine rotor components using powder metallurgy materials specified in 1C002.b.; or\n\n\nTechnical Note:\n\n\n'Damage tolerant' components are designed using methodology and substantiation to predict and limit crack growth.\n\n\n9.Not used;\n\n\n10.Not used;\n\n\n11.Hollow fan blades;\n\n\nb.\"Technology\" \"required\" for the \"development\" or \"production\" of any of the following:\n\n\n1.Wind tunnel aero-models equipped with non-intrusive sensors capable of transmitting data from the sensors to the data acquisition system; or\n\n\n2.\"Composite\" propeller blades or propfans, capable of absorbing more than 2000 kW at flight speeds exceeding Mach 0,55;\n\n\nc.\"Technology\" \"required\" for manufacturing cooling holes, in gas turbine engine components incorporating any of the \"technologies\" specified by 9E003.a.1., 9E003.a.2. or 9E003.a.5., and having any of the following:\n\n\n1.Having all of the following:\n\n\na.Minimum 'cross-sectional area' less than 0,45 mm2;\n\n\nb.'Hole shape ratio' greater than 4,52; and\n\n\n\n\nc.'Incidence angle' equal to or less than 25 \u00b0; or\n\n\n2.Having all of the following:\n\n\na.Minimum 'cross-sectional area' less than 0,12 mm2;\n\n\nb.'Hole shape ratio' greater than 5,65; and\n\n\nc.'Incidence angle' more than 25 \u00b0;\n\n\nNote:9E003.c. does not control \"technology\" for manufacturing constant radius cylindrical holes that are straight through and enter and exit on the external surfaces of the component.\n\n\nTechnical Notes:\n\n\n1.For the purposes of 9E003.c., the 'cross-sectional area' is the area of the hole in the plane perpendicular to the hole axis.\n\n\n2.For the purposes of 9E003.c., 'hole shape ratio' is the nominal length of the axis of the hole divided by the square root of its minimum 'cross-sectional area'.\n\n\n3.For the purposes of 9E003.c., 'incidence angle' is the acute angle measured between the plane tangential to the aerofoil surface and the hole axis at the point where the hole axis enters the aerofoil surface.\n\n\n4.Techniques for manufacturing holes in 9E003.c include \"laser\", water jet, Electro-Chemical Machining (ECM) or Electrical Discharge Machining (EDM) methods.\n\n\nd.\"Technology\" \"required\" for the \"development\" or \"production\" of helicopter power transfer systems or tilt rotor or tilt wing \"aircraft\" power transfer systems;\n\n\ne.\"Technology\" for the \"development\" or \"production\" of reciprocating diesel engine ground vehicle propulsion systems having all of the following:\n\n\n1.'Box volume' of 1,2 m3 or less;\n\n\n2.An overall power output of more than 750 kW based on 80/1269/EEC, ISO 2534 or national equivalents; and\n\n\n3.Power density of more than 700 kW/m3 of 'box volume';\n\n\nTechnical Note:\n\n\n'Box volume' in 9E003.e. is the product of three perpendicular dimensions measured in the following way:\n\n\n\n\n\nLength\n\n\n\n\n:\n\n\n\n\nThe length of the crankshaft from front flange to flywheel face;\n\n\n\n\n\n\nWidth\n\n\n\n\n:\n\n\n\n\nThe widest of any of the following:\n\n\na.The outside dimension from valve cover to valve cover;\n\n\nb.The dimensions of the outside edges of the cylinder heads; or\n\n\nc.The diameter of the flywheel housing;\n\n\n\n\n\n\nHeight\n\n\n\n\n:\n\n\n\n\nThe largest of any of the following:\n\n\na.The dimension of the crankshaft centre-line to the top plane of the valve cover (or cylinder head) plus twice the stroke; or\n\n\nb.The diameter of the flywheel housing.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nf.\"Technology\" \"required\" for the \"production\" of specially designed components for high output diesel engines, as follows:\n\n\n1.\"Technology\" \"required\" for the 1\u00a0\u00d6\u00a0\u2013\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Items\u00a0\u00d5\n\n\nThis general export authorisation covers all dual-use items specified in any entry in Section A of Annex I to this Regulation, Exporters that use this authorisation shall notify the competent authorities of the Member State where they are established of their first use of this authorisation no later than 30 days after the date when the first export took place.\n\n\nExporters shall also report in the Single Administrative Document the fact that they are using this authorisation EU 001 by indicating in box 44 the reference X002.\n\n\n2. This authorisation may not be used if:\n\n\n\u2013the exporter has been informed by the competent authorities of the Member State in which he is established that the items in question are or may be intended, in their entirety or in part, for use in connection with the development, production, handling, operation, maintenance, storage, detection, identification or dissemination of chemical, biological or nuclear weapons or other nuclear explosive devices or the development, production, maintenance or storage of missiles capable of delivering such weapons, or if the exporter is aware that the items in question are intended for such use;\n\n\n\u2013the exporter has been informed by the competent authorities of the Member State in which he is established that the items in question are or may be intended for a military end use as defined in Article 4(2) of this Regulation in a country subject to an arms embargo imposed by a decision or a common position adopted by the Council or a decision of the OSCE or an arms embargo imposed by a binding resolution of the Security Council of the United Nations, or if the exporter is aware that the items in question are intended for the above mentioned uses;\n\n\n\u2013the relevant items are exported to a customs free zone or free warehouse which is located in a destination covered by this authorisation.\n\n\n3. Reporting requirements attached to the use of this authorisation and the additional information that the Member State from which the export is made might require on items exported under this authorisation are defined by Member States.\n\n\nA Member State may require the exporters established in that Member State to register prior to the first use of this authorisation. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authorities to the exporter without delay and in any case within ten working days of receipt.\n\n\nWhere applicable the requirements set out in the first two paragraphs of this point shall be based on those defined for the use of national general export authorisations granted by those Member States which provide for such authorisations.\n\n\n\n\u00f2\u00a0new\n\n\n1This authorisation may not be used if:\n\n\n\n\n(1)the exporter has been informed by the competent authority of the Member State in which he is resident or established that the items in question are or may be intended, in their entirety or in part, for use in connection with the development, production, handling, operation, maintenance, storage, detection, identification or dissemination of chemical, biological or nuclear weapons or other nuclear explosive devices or the development, production, maintenance or storage of missiles capable of delivering such weapons, or if the exporter is aware that the items in question are intended for such use;\n\n\n(2)the exporter has been informed by the competent authority of the Member State in which he is resident or established that the items in question are or may be intended for a military end use, or if the exporter is aware that the items in question are intended for the above mentioned use;\n\n\n(3)the relevant items are exported to a customs free zone or free warehouse which is located in a destination covered by this authorisation.\n\n\n2.Exporters shall declare that the items are being exported under Union General Export Authorisation EU001 in the customs declaration.\n\n\n3.Any exporter intending to use this authorisation shall register prior to the first use of this authorisation with the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the exporter within ten working days of receipt.\n\n\n4.The registered exporter shall notify the first use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established, no later than 10 days before the date of the first export. \n\n\n5.The registered exporter shall report to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established on the use of this authorisation. The report on the use of this authorisation shall be produced at least once per year and shall include at least the following information: \n\n\n(1)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(2)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(3)the name and address of the consignee; \n\n\n(4)where known, the end-use and end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\n\n\u00ea\u00a02420/2015 Art. 1.2 and Annex II (adapted)\n\n\n\u00f0\u00a0new\n\n\nANNEX IIb\n\n\n\u00d6\u00a0B.EXPORTS OF CERTAIN DUAL-USE ITEMS TO Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authorities to the exporter without delay and in any case within 10 working days of receipt, subject to Article 9(1) of this Regulation.\n\n\nWhere applicable the requirements set out in the second and third paragraphs shall be based on those defined for the use of national general export authorisations granted by those Member States which provide for such authorisations.\n\n\n\n\u00f2\u00a0new\n\n\n3.Any exporter intending to use this authorisation shall register prior to the first use of this authorisation with the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the exporter within 10 working days of receipt.\n\n\n4.The registered exporter shall notify the first use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established, no later than 10 days before the date of the first export.\n\n\n5.The registered exporter shall report to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established on the use of this authorisation. The report on the use of this authorisation shall be produced at least once per year and shall include at least the following information: \n\n\n(1)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(2)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(3)the name and address of the consignee; \n\n\n(4)where known, the end-use and end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\n\n\u00ea\u00a02420/2015 Art. 1.2 and Annex II (adapted)\n\n\n\u00f0\u00a0new\n\n\nANNEX IIc\n\n\n\u00d6\u00a0C.EXPORT AFTER or\n\n\n\n\n(c)for use as parts or components of military items listed in the national military list that have been exported from the territory of the Member State concerned without authorisation or in breach of an authorisation prescribed by the national legislation of that Member State;\n\n\n(2)the exporter is aware that the items in question are intended, in their entirety or in part, for any of the uses referred to in subparagraph (1);\n\n\n(3)the relevant items are exported to a customs-free zone or a free warehouse which is located in a destination covered by this authorisation;\n\n\n(4)the initial authorisation has been annulled, suspended, modified or revoked;\n\n\n(5)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the end-use of the items in question is different from that specified in the original export authorisation.\n\n\n3.On exportation of any of the items pursuant to this authorisation, exporters \u00d6\u00a0shall\u00a0\u00d5\u00a0must:\n\n\n(1)mention the reference number of the initial export authorisation in the export declaration to customs together with the name of the Member State that granted the authorisation, the EU reference number X002 and specify\u00a0\u00d6\u00a0declare\u00a0\u00d5 that the items are being exported under Union General Export Authorisation EU003 in box 44 of the \u00d6\u00a0customs declaration\u00a0\u00d5\u00a0Single Administrative Document;\n\n\n(2)provide customs officers, if so requested, with documentary evidence of the date of importation of the items into the Union, of any maintenance, repair or replacement of the items carried out in the Union and of the fact that the items are being returned to the end-user and the country from which they were imported into the Union.\n\n\n4. or\n\n\n(c)for use as parts or components of military items listed in the national military list that have been exported from the territory of the Member State concerned without authorisation or in breach of an authorisation prescribed by the national legislation of that Member State;\n\n\n(2)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the items in question are intended, in their entirety or in part, for any of the uses referred to in subparagraph 1;\n\n\n(3)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the items in question will be re-exported to any destination other than those listed in Part 2 of this Annex\u00a0Section or in Part 2 of Annex IIa\u00a0Section A of this Annex\u00a0or to\u00a0and the Member States; Any exporter who uses this authorisation must notify the competent authorities of the Member State where he is established of the first use of this authorisation no later than 30 days after the date when the first export took place or, alternatively, and in accordance with a requirement by the competent authority of the Member State where the exporter is established, prior to the first use of this authorisation. Member States shall notify the Commission of the notification mechanism chosen for this authorisation. The Commission shall publish the information notified to it in the C series of the Official Journal of the European Union.\n\n\nReporting requirements attached to the use of this authorisation and additional information that the Member State from which the export is made might require on items exported under this authorisation are defined by Member States.\n\n\nA Member State may require exporters established in that Member State to register prior to the first use of this authorisation. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authorities to the exporter without delay and in any case within 10 working days of receipt, subject to Article 9(1) of this Regulation.\n\n\nWhere applicable the requirements set out in the second and third subparagraphs shall be based on those defined for the use of national general export authorisations granted by those Member States which provide for such authorisations.\n\n\n\n\u00f2\u00a0new\n\n\n3.Any exporter intending to use this authorisation shall register prior to the first use of this authorisation with the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the exporter within 10 working days of receipt.\n\n\n4.The registered exporter shall notify the first use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established, no later than 10 days before the date of the first export.\n\n\n5.The registered exporter shall report to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established on the use of this authorisation. A single export order broken down into a number of shipments constitutes one low value shipment.\n\n\n2.This authorisation does not authorise the export of items where:\n\n\n(1)the exporter has been informed by the competent authority of the Member State in which he is resident or established that the items in question are or may be intended, in their entirety or in part:\n\n\n\n\n(a)for use in connection with the development, production, handling, operation, maintenance, storage, detection, identification or dissemination of chemical, biological or nuclear weapons or other nuclear explosive devices, or the development, production, maintenance or storage of missiles capable of delivering such weapons;\n\n\n(b)for a military end-use;\n\n\n(c)for use as parts or components of military items listed in the national military list that have been exported from the territory of the Member State concerned without authorisation or in breach of an authorisation prescribed by the national legislation of that Member State; \n\n\n(2)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the items in question are intended, in their entirety or in part, for any of the uses referred to in subparagraph 1;\n\n\n(3)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the items in question will be re-exported to any destination other than those listed in Part 2 of Section A of this Annex and the Member States;\n\n\n(4)the relevant items are exported to a customs-free zone or a free warehouse which is located in a destination covered by this authorisation.\n\n\n3.Orders may not be split to meet the value limit. \n\n\n4.The total value of exports per calendar year from the same exporter to the same consignee or end-user of items listed under a single control entry in Part 1 may not exceed twelve times the value limit set in this authorisation. \n\n\n5.Exporters shall declare that the items are being exported under Union General Export Authorisation EU007 in the customs declaration.\n\n\n6.Any exporter intending to use this authorisation shall register prior to the first use of this authorisation with the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the exporter within 10 working days of receipt.\n\n\n7.The registered exporter shall notify the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established of the first use of this authorisation no later than 10 days before the date of the first export.\n\n\n8.The registered exporter shall report to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established on the use of this authorisation. The report on the use of this authorisation shall be produced at least once per year and shall include at least the following information: \n\n\n(1)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(2)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(3)the name and address of the consignee; \n\n\n(4)where known, the end-use and end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\n9.Exporters who have not used this authorisation within a 24-month period automatically lose to their entitlement to use this authorisation.\n\n\n10.For the purposes of this authorisation, 'low value shipment' means items which are comprised in a single export order and are dispatched by an exporter to a named consignee in one or more consignments, the aggregate value of which does not exceed EUR 5 000. For this purpose 'value' means the price billed to the consignee, except for the shipping charges and the value of items that are not listed in Part 1. \n\n\n\n\nH. INTRA-COMPANY TRANSMISSION OF SOFTWARE AND TECHNOLOGY\n\n\nUNION GENERAL EXPORT AUTHORISATION NO EU008\n\n\n\n\n(referred to in Article 10(1)(d) of this Regulation)\n\n\nIntra-company transmission of software and technology\n\n\nIssuing authority: European Union\n\n\nPart 1 \u2013\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Items\n\n\nThis general export authorisation covers all technology and software specified in Section A of Annex I to this Regulation, except those listed in Section K of this Annex. \n\n\nPart 2 \u2013\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Destinations\n\n\nThis authorisation is valid throughout the Union for the transmission of software and technology to all destinations, excluding those subject to an arms embargo and those subject to restrictive measures of the Union applicable to dual-use goods and technology.\n\n\nPart 3 \u2013\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Conditions and requirements for use\n\n\n1.This authorisation authorises the transmission of software and technology listed in Part 1 by any exporter resident or established in a Member State of the Union provided the item is only for use:\n\n\n(1)by the exporter or by any entity owned or controlled by the exporter; \n\n\n(2)by employees of the exporter or of any entity owned or controlled by the exporter\n\n\nin its or their own commercial product development activities and, in the case of employees, pursuant to the agreement establishing the employment relationship.\n\n\n2.This authorisation does not authorise the transmission of software and technology where:\n\n\n(1)the exporter has been informed by the competent authority of the Member State in which it is resident or established that the software and technology in question are or may be intended, in their entirety or in part:\n\n\n(a)for use in connection with the development, production, handling, operation, maintenance, storage, detection, identification or dissemination of chemical, biological or nuclear weapons or other nuclear explosive devices, or the development, production, maintenance or storage of missiles capable of delivering such weapons;\n\n\n(b)for a military end-use;\n\n\n(2)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the software and technology in question are intended, in their entirety or in part, for any of the uses referred to in subparagraph 1;\n\n\n(3)the exporter, under his obligation to exercise due diligence, is aware that the software and technology in question will be re-transmitted to any destination other than those listed in Part 2 of Section A of this Annex and the Member States.\n\n\n3.Any exporter intending to use this authorisation shall implement an 'Internal Compliance Programme'.\n\n\n4.Exporters shall declare that the items are being exported under Union General Export Authorisation EU008 in the customs declaration in the case of tangible export of software.\n\n\n\n\n5.Any exporter intending to use this authorisation shall register prior to the first use of this authorisation with the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the exporter within 10 working days of receipt.\n\n\nThe registered exporter shall notify the first use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established, no later than 10 days before the date of the first export. \n\n\n6.The registered exporter using this authorisation shall report to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established on the use of this authorisation. The report on the use of this authorisation shall be produced at least once per year and shall include at least the following information: \n\n\n(1)the description of the dual-use software and technology, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(2)the name and address of the end-user of the dual-use software and technology.\n\n\n\n\nI. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the exporter within 10 working days of receipt. \n\n\n4.The registered exporter shall notify the first use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established, no later than 10 days before the date of the first export. \n\n\n5.The registered exporter shall report to the competent authority of the Member State where he is resident or established on the use of this authorisation. The report on the use of this authorisation shall be produced at least once per year and shall include at least the following information: \n\n\n(1)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(2)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(3)the name and address of the consignee; \n\n\n(4)where known, the end-use and end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\n\n\u00ea\u00a02420/2015 Art. 1.2 and Annex II (adapted)\n\n\n\u00f0\u00a0new\n\n\nANNEX IIg\n\n\nK.\u00a0(List referred to in Article 910(46)(a) of this Regulation and Section A, C, D,\u00a0\u00f0\u00a0G and H\u00a0\u00ef\u00a0of this Annexes\u00a0IIa, IIc and IId to this Regulation)\n\n\nThe entries do not always provide a complete description of the items and the related notes in Section A of Annex I. Registration shall be automatic and acknowledged by the competent authority to the operator within 10 working days of receipt.\n\n\n3.The registered operator shall notify the first use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State from which the dual-use items are to be transferred, no later than 10 days before the date of the first transfer. \n\n\n4.The registered operator using this authorisation to transfer items listed Part I of Section B of this Annex shall report on the use of this authorisation to the competent authority of the Member State from which the dual-use items are to be transferred. The report on the use of this authorisation shall be produced, at least, once per year and shall, at least, include the following information: \n\n\n(1)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(2)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(3)the name and address of the consignee; \n\n\n(4)where known, the end-use and end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\n5.The registered operator using this authorisation to transfer items listed Part II of Section B of this Annex shall transmit to the competent authority of the Member State from which the dual-use items are to be transferred no later than 20 days after the end of each quarter a report specifying for each transfer, at least, the following information:\n\n\n\n\n(1)the date of transfer; \n\n\n(2)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(3)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(4)the location, name, and address of the end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\nIn this context, a quarter means a period of three consecutive months starting on January 1, April 1, July 1 or October 1.\n\n\n6.The registered operator using this authorisation to transfer items listed in Part III of Section B of this Annex shall notify the competent authority of the Member State from which the dual-use items are to be transferred no later than 10 days prior to each transfer, at least, the following information:\n\n\n(1)the date of transfer; \n\n\n(2)the description of the dual-use items, including the relevant control entry from Section A of Annex I to this Regulation;\n\n\n(3)the quantity and the value of the dual-use items;\n\n\n(4)the location, name, and address of the end-user of the dual-use items.\n\n\n7.Member States shall notify the Commission of any additional reporting requirements attached to the use of this authorisation. The Commission shall publish the information notified to it in the C series of the Official Journal of the European Union.\n\n\n8.The competent authority of the Member State from which a transfer was made may request confirmation from the competent authority in the recipient Member State that an item or items transferred by a particular operator have been received by the intended end-user. \n\n\n9.The competent authority of the Member State from which a transfer was made may request the competent authority in the recipient Member State to conduct a post-shipment inspection of the item or items transferred to the intended end-user.\n\n\n10.The competent authority of the Member State from which the dual-use items are to be transferred can prohibit the operator from using this authorisation if there is reasonable suspicion about his ability to comply with the conditions and requirements of use of this authorisation. When performing such an assessment, the competent authority of the Member State from which the dual-use items are to be transferred shall consult with the competent authority of the Member State where the operator is established.\n\n\n11.The competent authorities of the Member States shall exchange information on operators deprived of the right to use this authorisation. The system referred to in Article 20(3) shall be used for this purpose.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nB. List of dual-use items subject to Union transfer authorisation referred to in Article 12 of this Regulation\n\n\nThe entries do not always cover the complete description of the item and the related notes in Section A of Annex I\n14\n. Only Section A of Annex I provides for the complete description of the items.\n\n\nThe mention of an item in this Annex does not affect the application of the provisions concerning mass-market products in Section A of Annex I.\n\n\nExemptions:\n\n\n\n\nThis Annex does not control the following items of the MTCR technology:\n\n\n1.that are transferred on the basis of orders pursuant to a contractual relationship placed by the European Space Agency (ESA) or that are transferred by ESA to accomplish its official tasks;\n\n\n2.that are transferred on the basis of orders pursuant to a contractual relationship placed by a Member State's national space organisation or that are transferred by it to accomplish its official tasks;\n\n\n3.that are transferred on the basis of orders pursuant to a contractual relationship placed in connection with a Union space launch development and production programme signed by two or more European governments;\n\n\n4.that are transferred to a State-controlled space launching site in the territory of a Member State, unless that Member State controls such transfers within the terms of this Regulation.\n\n\nThis Annex does not control the following items of the NSG Part 1 and Part 2 technology:\n\n\n1.that are transferred by the Euratom or IAEA safeguards inspectorates in the performance of their official tasks;\n\n\n2.that are transferred on the basis of orders pursuant to a contractual relationship placed by the Euratom or IAEA safeguards inspectorate.\n\n\nThis Annex does not control the following items of the NSG Part 2 technology:\n\n\n1.that are transferred on the basis of orders placed by the ITER International Fusion Energy Organisation pursuant to a contractual relationship or that are transferred by it to accomplish its official tasks;\n\n\n2.that are transferred on the basis of orders placed by the European Joint Undertaking for ITER and the Development of Fusion Energy\u00a0pursuant to a contractual relationship or that are transferred by it to accomplish its official tasks.\n\n\n\nPART I\n\n\nItems of stealth technology\n\n\n\n\n\n1E101\n\n\n\n\n\"Technology\" according to the GTN for the II\n\n\nItems listed in NSG Part 1\n\n\nUnless otherwise indicated, a reference in the table below to an entry includes all sub entries to that entry.\n\n\n\n\n\n0A001\n\n\n\n\n\"Nuclear reactors\" and specially designed or prepared equipment and components therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0B003\n\n\n\n\nPlant for the conversion of uranium and equipment specially designed or prepared therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0B005\n\n\n\n\nPlant specially designed for the fabrication of \"nuclear reactor\" fuel elements and specially designed or prepared equipment therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0C004\n\n\n\n\nGraphite having a purity level better than 5 parts per million 'boron equivalent' and with a density greater than 1,50 g/cm3 for use in a \"nuclear reactor\", in quantities exceeding 1 kg.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nPART III\n\n\nItems of the CWC (Chemical Weapons Convention)\n\n\n\n\n\n1C351.d.4.\n\n\n\n\nRicin\n\n\n\n\n\n\n1C351.d.5.\n\n\n\n\nSaxitoxin\n\n\n\n\n\nItems of the NSG Part 1 technology\n\n\nUnless otherwise indicated, a reference in the table below to an entry includes all sub entries to that entry.\n\n\n\n\n\n0B001\n\n\n\n\nPlant for the separation of isotopes of \"natural uranium\", \"depleted uranium\" and \"special fissile materials\", and specially designed or prepared equipment and components therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0B002\n\n\n\n\nSpecially designed or prepared auxiliary systems, equipment and components for isotope separation plant specified in 0B001, made of or protected by \"materials resistant to corrosion by UF6\".\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0B004\n\n\n\n\nPlant for the production or concentration of heavy water, deuterium and deuterium compounds and specially designed or prepared equipment and components therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0B006\n\n\n\n\nPlant for the reprocessing of irradiated \"nuclear reactor\" fuel elements, and specially designed or prepared equipment and components therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0B007\n\n\n\n\nPlant for the conversion of plutonium and equipment specially designed or prepared therefor.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0C002\n\n\n\n\nThis item is not included in Section B of Annex IV, with the exception of \"special fissile materials\" as follows: \n\n\na. Separated plutonium;\n\n\nb. \"Uranium enriched in the isotopes 235 or 233\" to more than 20%.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0C003\n\n\n\n\nDeuterium, heavy water (deuterium oxide) and other compounds of deuterium, and mixtures and solutions containing deuterium, in which the isotopic ratio of deuterium to hydrogen exceeds 1:5 000. \n\n\nN.B.: 0C003 is included in Section B of Annex IV only if for use in a \"nuclear reactor\" (within 0A001.a.).\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0D001\n\n\n\n\n(software) is included in Section B of Annex IV in respect of all items of Category 0 listed in Part III.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n0E001\n\n\n\n\n(technology) is included in Section B of Annex IV in respect of all items of Category 0 listed in Part III.\n\n\n\n\n\n\nItems of the NSG Part 2 technology\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n6A203\n\n\n\n\nCameras and components, other than those specified in 6A003, as follows:\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0a. Mechanical rotating mirror cameras, as follows, and specially designed components therefor:\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a01. Framing cameras with recording rates greater than 225 000 frames per second;\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a02. Streak cameras with writing speeds greater than 0,5\u00a0mm per microsecond;\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0Note: In 6A203.a. components of such cameras include their synchronizing electronics units and rotor assemblies consisting of turbines, mirrors and bearings.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n6A225\n\n\n\n\nVelocity interferometers for measuring velocities exceeding 1\u00a0km/s during time intervals of less than 10 microseconds.\n\n\nNote: 6A225 includes velocity interferometers such as VISARs (Velocity interferometer systems for any reflector) and DLIs (Doppler laser interferometers).\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n6A226\n\n\n\n\nPressure sensors, as follows:\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0a. Manganin gauges for pressures greater than 10 GPa;\n\n\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0b. Quartz pressure transducers for pressures greater than 10 GPa.\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\u00ea\u00a0428/2009 (adapted)\n\n\n\u00e81\u00a0Corrigendum, OJ L 224, 27.8.2009, p. 21\n\n\nANNEX V\n\n\nRepealed
